                </span>
               </a>
              </li>
             </ul>

         <div itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Article">
          <meta content="2014-08-15T18:09:36Z" itemprop="datePublished"/>
          <meta content="Road &amp; Track" itemprop="provider"/>
          <meta content="Not just one, but 200 barn finds go to auction" itemprop="headline"/>
          <meta content="Alex Kierstein" itemprop="author"/>
          <meta content="The Bullock Family collection goes under the hammer in Nebraska." itemprop="description"/>
          <meta content="https://s.yimg.com/os/publish-images/autos/2014-08-13/ea20ebf0-2341-11e4-99ef-2b77057e0c3c_Bullock_06_2000.jpg" itemprop="image"/>
          <div class="yom-mod yom-art-content " id="mediaarticlebody" itemprop="articleBody">
           <div class="bd">
            <!-- google_ad_section_start -->
            <div class="hotdog" style="margin:10px;padding:5px 0px;border-top:5px solid #e4e5e4;border-bottom:5px solid #e4e4e4;width:255px;float:right;clear:both;display:inline;">
             <h4 style="margin:3px 0px 8px 5px;padding:0px;font-size:10px;font-weight:bold;font-family:verdana;color:#555555;text-transform:uppercase;">
              MORE AT ROAD &amp; TRACK
             </h4>
             <ul style="margin:3px;padding:0px;list-style-type:none;font-family:verdana;font-size:10px;">
              <li style="margin:0px 0px 6px 3px;padding:0px;list-style-type:none;list-style-position:inside;">
               <em style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;color:#db612d;">
                
               </em>
               <a href="https://us.lrd.yahoo.com/_ylt=AwrTV7oKqKFVSwMAYgN3HmRH;_ylu=X3oDMTFqMDgxZXM0BG1pdANBcnRpY2xlIEJvZHkEcG9zAzEEc2VjA01lZGlhQXJ0aWNsZUJvZHlBc3NlbWJseQ--;_ylg=X3oDMTJuMnU2OHY5BGludGwDY2EEbGFuZwNlbi1jYQRwc3RhaWQDZTAzYjZlNjktMzMzNi0zYTUyLThlZjAtNDQyMzNmMjJhYWEzBHBzdGNhdANuZXdzBHB0A3N0b3J5cGFnZQ--;_ylv=0/SIG=158jo1quh/EXP=1437867274/**http%3A//www.roadandtrack.com/go/car-culture/the-curious-history-behind-the-garage-find-gt40%3Flink=rel%26amp;dom=yah_auto%26amp;src=syn%26amp;mag=rat" style="color:#1053fc;text-decoration:none;" target="_blank">
                The Curious History of the Garage-Find Ford GT40
               </a>
              </li>
              <li style="margin:0px 0px 6px 3px;padding:0px;list-style-type:none;list-style-position:inside;">
               <em style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;color:#db612d;">
                
               </em>
               <a href="https://us.lrd.yahoo.com/_ylt=AwrTV7oKqKFVSwMAYwN3HmRH;_ylu=X3oDMTFqaWd2Ymg3BG1pdANBcnRpY2xlIEJvZHkEcG9zAzIEc2VjA01lZGlhQXJ0aWNsZUJvZHlBc3NlbWJseQ--;_ylg=X3oDMTJuMnU2OHY5BGludGwDY2EEbGFuZwNlbi1jYQRwc3RhaWQDZTAzYjZlNjktMzMzNi0zYTUyLThlZjAtNDQyMzNmMjJhYWEzBHBzdGNhdANuZXdzBHB0A3N0b3J5cGFnZQ--;_ylv=0/SIG=15d7qvmtb/EXP=1437867274/**http%3A//www.roadandtrack.com/car-videos/latest/ford-mustang-burnout-drift-fail-video-compliation%3Flink=rel%26amp;dom=yah_auto%26amp;src=syn%26amp;mag=rat" style="color:#1053fc;text-decoration:none;" target="_blank">
                Mustang Drivers Show How NOT to Leave a Car Show
               </a>
              </li>
              <li style="margin:0px 0px 6px 3px;padding:0px;list-style-type:none;list-style-position:inside;">
               <em style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;color:#db612d;">
                
               </em>
               <a href="https://us.lrd.yahoo.com/_ylt=AwrTV7oKqKFVSwMAZAN3HmRH;_ylu=X3oDMTFqaTNjbzlmBG1pdANBcnRpY2xlIEJvZHkEcG9zAzMEc2VjA01lZGlhQXJ0aWNsZUJvZHlBc3NlbWJseQ--;_ylg=X3oDMTJuMnU2OHY5BGludGwDY2EEbGFuZwNlbi1jYQRwc3RhaWQDZTAzYjZlNjktMzMzNi0zYTUyLThlZjAtNDQyMzNmMjJhYWEzBHBzdGNhdANuZXdzBHB0A3N0b3J5cGFnZQ--;_ylv=0/SIG=1588fshil/EXP=1437867274/**http%3A//www.roadandtrack.com/car-reviews/car-comparison-tests/photos-12-best-cars-under-30k%3Flink=rel%26amp;dom=yah_auto%26amp;src=syn%26amp;mag=rat" style="color:#1053fc;text-decoration:none;" target="_blank">
                12 Best Cars You Can Buy Under $30K
               </a>
              </li>
             </ul>
            </div>
            <p class="first">
             VanDerBrink Auctions of Minnesota has managed to ferret out one of those legendary
             <a href="https://us.lrd.yahoo.com/_ylt=AwrTV7oKqKFVSwMAZQN3HmRH;_ylu=X3oDMTFqc2Fobm1zBG1pdANBcnRpY2xlIEJvZHkEcG9zAzQEc2VjA01lZGlhQXJ0aWNsZUJvZHlBc3NlbWJseQ--;_ylg=X3oDMTJuMnU2OHY5BGludGwDY2EEbGFuZwNlbi1jYQRwc3RhaWQDZTAzYjZlNjktMzMzNi0zYTUyLThlZjAtNDQyMzNmMjJhYWEzBHBzdGNhdANuZXdzBHB0A3N0b3J5cGFnZQ--;_ylv=0/SIG=14991dp0q/EXP=1437867274/**http%3A//www.roadandtrack.com/rt-archive/barn-finds-revisited%3Flink=rel%26amp;dom=yah_auto%26amp;src=syn%26amp;mag=rat" target="_blank">
              barn find situations
             </a>
             in Nebraska. And it's not just one car, it's about 200 of them, plus an unquantifiable amount of parts. It has all the hallmarks of a romantic barn find story: a family collection, photos of dust-caked American iron, the possibility of an immensely rare model hiding next to the vanilla sedans.
             <br/>
             <br/>
             The Bullocks acquired the massive collection as a necessary part of the restoration business they ran in addition to the dealership. Also, some cars that they'd sold were traded back to them. Among the forgettable filler are a couple gems: there's a restored 1967 Pontiac GTO coupe, a restored 1937 Diamond T pickup  and so on, and so forth. The PDF of the auction catalog runs to 121 pages. Boats, campers, NOS parts from the 1930sit's almost overwhelming.
             <br/>
             <br/>
             Everything is no reserve, so if you're itching to sniff out the really good stuff from underneath all that dust, you can head to Grant, Nebraska on September 6th.
             <br/>
             <br/>
             <span class="yom-figure yom-fig-middle" style="width:630px;">
              <a href="https://autos.yahoo.com/photos/the-bullock-collection-from-the-vanderbrink-auctions-1407972795-slideshow/;_ylt=AwrTV7oKqKFVSwMAZgN3HmRH;_ylu=X3oDMTFqaGFmbHBnBG1pdANBcnRpY2xlIEJvZHkEcG9zAzUEc2VjA01lZGlhQXJ0aWNsZUJvZHlBc3NlbWJseQ--;_ylg=X3oDMTJuMnU2OHY5BGludGwDY2EEbGFuZwNlbi1jYQRwc3RhaWQDZTAzYjZlNjktMzMzNi0zYTUyLThlZjAtNDQyMzNmMjJhYWEzBHBzdGNhdANuZXdzBHB0A3N0b3J5cGFnZQ--">
               <img alt="Chevrolet Impala SS convertible" class="editorial" src="https://s1.yimg.com/bt/api/res/1.2/LyRe3wQrRJMcWDTQPBQv4A--/YXBwaWQ9eW5ld3M7cT04NTt3PTYzMA--/http://l.yimg.com/os/publish-images/autos/2014-08-13/5a2c4500-233f-11e4-a021-efb632dc6dd9_Bullock_04_2000.jpg" title="Chevrolet Impala SS convertible" width="630"/>
              </a>
              <span class="legend">
               Chevrolet Impala SS convertible
              </span>
             </span>
            </p>
            <div class="yom-fig-frame" style="width:100%;text-align:center;margin:auto;">
